Grammar Runner.Language.grammar.y - 3/1/2018 4:53:12 PM

    1 $accept: main EOF
             ;

    2 main: statements_and_declarations
    3     | /* empty */
          ;

    4 statements_and_declarations: statement_or_declaration
    5                            | statements_and_declarations statement_or_declaration
                                 ;

    6 statement_or_declaration: statement
    7                         | function_declaration
                              ;

    8 statements: statement
    9           | statements statement
                ;

   10 statement: block
   11          | while
   12          | dowhile
   13          | for
   14          | if
   15          | return
   16          | variable_declaration SEMICOLON
   17          | statement_expression SEMICOLON
               ;

   18 expression: statement_expression
   19           | function_expression
   20           | function_named_expression
                ;

   21 statement_expression: assignment
   22                     | conditional
   23                     | comma
   24                     | binary_valid_expression
                          ;

   25 binary_valid_expression: arithmetic
   26                        | indexer_expression
   27                        | comparison
   28                        | bitwise
   29                        | unary
   30                        | logical
   31                        | delete
   32                        | typeof
   33                        | void
   34                        | in
   35                        | instanceof
                             ;

   36 invocation_expression: function_expression
   37                      | function_named_expression
                           ;

   38 unary_expression: indexer_expression
   39                 | invocation_expression
   40                 | function_invocation_func
                      ;

   41 indexer_expression: lvalue
   42                   | NUMBER
   43                   | STRING
   44                   | boolean
   45                   | array
   46                   | object
   47                   | function_invocation
   48                   | LPARENTH expression RPARENTH
                        ;

   49 lvalue: IDENTIFIER
   50       | property_getter
   51       | indexer_getter
            ;

   52 block: LCURLYBRACE RCURLYBRACE
   53      | LCURLYBRACE statements RCURLYBRACE
           ;

   54 statement_or_semicolon: statement
   55                       | SEMICOLON
                            ;

   56 function_declaration: FUNCTION IDENTIFIER LPARENTH arguments_list 
                                RPARENTH function_body
                          ;

   57 function_expression: FUNCTION LPARENTH arguments_list RPARENTH 
                               function_body
                         ;

   58 function_named_expression: FUNCTION IDENTIFIER LPARENTH 
                                     arguments_list RPARENTH function_body
                               ;

   59 function_body: LCURLYBRACE RCURLYBRACE
   60              | LCURLYBRACE statements_and_declarations RCURLYBRACE
                   ;

   61 return: RETURN SEMICOLON
   62       | RETURN expression SEMICOLON
            ;

   63 arguments_list: IDENTIFIER
   64               | arguments_list COMMA IDENTIFIER
   65               | /* empty */
                    ;

   66 while: WHILE LPARENTH expression RPARENTH statement_or_semicolon
           ;

   67 dowhile: DO block WHILE LPARENTH expression RPARENTH SEMICOLON
             ;

   68 for: FOR LPARENTH expression_or_empty SEMICOLON expression_or_empty 
               SEMICOLON expression_or_empty RPARENTH statement_or_semicolon
         ;

   69 expression_or_empty: expression
   70                    | /* empty */
                         ;

   71 if: IF LPARENTH expression RPARENTH statement_or_semicolon
   72   | IF LPARENTH expression RPARENTH statement_or_semicolon ELSE 
            statement_or_semicolon
        ;

   73 variable_declaration: VAR variable_declaration_identifier
   74                     | variable_declaration COMMA variable_declaration_identifier
                          ;

   75 variable_declaration_identifier: IDENTIFIER
   76                                | IDENTIFIER ASSIGN expression
                                     ;

   77 boolean: TRUE
   78        | FALSE
             ;

   79 array: LBRACKET array_list RBRACKET
   80      | LBRACKET RBRACKET
           ;

   81 array_list: expression
   82           | array_list COMMA expression
                ;

   83 object: LCURLYBRACE object_properties_list RCURLYBRACE
            ;

   84 object_properties_list: object_property
   85                       | object_property COMMA object_properties_list
                            ;

   86 object_property: object_property_identifier COLON expression
                     ;

   87 object_property_identifier: IDENTIFIER
   88                           | STRING
                                ;

   89 function_invocation: indexer_expression LPARENTH 
                               function_invocation_arguments_list RPARENTH
                         ;

   90 function_invocation_func: invocation_expression LPARENTH 
                                    function_invocation_arguments_list 
                                    RPARENTH
                              ;

   91 function_invocation_arguments_list: expression
   92                                   | function_invocation_arguments_list COMMA expression
   93                                   | /* empty */
                                        ;

   94 indexer_getter: indexer_expression LBRACKET expression RBRACKET
                    ;

   95 property_getter: indexer_expression DOT IDENTIFIER
                     ;

   96 assignment: lvalue ASSIGN expression
   97           | lvalue ADDASSG expression
   98           | lvalue SUBASSG expression
   99           | lvalue MULTASSG expression
  100           | lvalue DIVASSG expression
  101           | lvalue REMASSG expression
  102           | lvalue EXPASSG expression
  103           | lvalue LEFTSHFTASG expression
  104           | lvalue RIGHTSHFTASSG expression
  105           | lvalue URIGHTSHFTASSG expression
  106           | lvalue BITWISEANDASSG expression
  107           | lvalue BITWISEXORASSG expression
  108           | lvalue BITWISEORASSG expression
                ;

  109 comparison: binary_valid_expression EQUAL binary_valid_expression
  110           | binary_valid_expression NOTEQUAL binary_valid_expression
  111           | binary_valid_expression STRICTEQUAL binary_valid_expression
  112           | binary_valid_expression STRICTNOTEQUAL binary_valid_expression
  113           | binary_valid_expression GREATERTHAN binary_valid_expression
  114           | binary_valid_expression GREATERTHANOREQUAL binary_valid_expression
  115           | binary_valid_expression LESSTHAN binary_valid_expression
  116           | binary_valid_expression LESSTHANOREQUAL binary_valid_expression
                ;

  117 arithmetic: binary_valid_expression ADDITION binary_valid_expression
  118           | binary_valid_expression SUBTRACTION binary_valid_expression
  119           | binary_valid_expression MULTIPLICATION binary_valid_expression
  120           | binary_valid_expression DIVISION binary_valid_expression
  121           | binary_valid_expression REMAINDER indexer_expression
  122           | binary_valid_expression EXPONENTIATION binary_valid_expression
                ;

  123 unary: BITWISENOT unary_expression
  124      | ADDITION unary_expression
  125      | SUBTRACTION unary_expression
  126      | INCREMENT lvalue
  127      | lvalue INCREMENT
  128      | DECREMENT lvalue
  129      | lvalue DECREMENT
  130      | LOGICALNOT unary_expression
           ;

  131 bitwise: binary_valid_expression BITWISEAND binary_valid_expression
  132        | binary_valid_expression BITWISEOR binary_valid_expression
  133        | binary_valid_expression BITWISEXOR binary_valid_expression
  134        | binary_valid_expression LEFTSHIFT binary_valid_expression
  135        | binary_valid_expression SIGNPROPRIGHTSHIFT binary_valid_expression
  136        | binary_valid_expression ZEROFILLRIGHTSHIFT binary_valid_expression
             ;

  137 logical: binary_valid_expression LOGICALAND binary_valid_expression
  138        | binary_valid_expression LOGICALOR binary_valid_expression
             ;

  139 conditional: statement_expression QUESTION statement_expression COLON 
                       statement_expression
                 ;

  140 comma: binary_valid_expression COMMA binary_valid_expression
           ;

  141 delete: DELETE lvalue
            ;

  142 typeof: TYPEOF expression
            ;

  143 void: VOID expression
          ;

  144 in: binary_valid_expression IN binary_valid_expression
        ;

  145 instanceof: binary_valid_expression INSTANCEOF 
                      binary_valid_expression
                ;
